### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_Short` — TDEF page 25

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **1**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_Long` — TDEF page 27

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **1**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_IEEESingle` — TDEF page 29

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **1**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

| Section | Start | Size | End (excl) |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Page header | 0 | 8 | 8 |

| Column descriptors (numCols × 25) | 63 | 25 | 88 |
| Column names (length-prefixed) | 88 | 12 | 100 |
| Variable trailing block (per-var-col page ptrs) | (after names) | (variable, terminated by col_num=0xFFFF) | — |

### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_IEEEDouble` — TDEF page 31

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **1**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

### Section offsets (computed)

| Section | Start | Size | End (excl) |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Page header | 0 | 8 | 8 |
| TDEF block (Jet4: 55 bytes) | 8 | 55 | 63 |
| Real-idx skip entries (numRealIdx × 12) | 63 | 0 | 63 |
| Column descriptors (numCols × 25) | 63 | 25 | 88 |
| Column names (length-prefixed) | 88 | 12 | 100 |
| Variable trailing block (per-var-col page ptrs) | (after names) | (variable, terminated by col_num=0xFFFF) | — |

### Column descriptors

| # | Name | Type (hex) | Type meaning | col_num | offset_F | col_len | flags (hex) | misc (hex, 4 bytes) |
|---:|---|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---|---|
| 0 | `Value` | 0x07 | DOUBLE | 0 | 0 | 8 | 0x03 | `09 04 00 00` |

### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_GUID` — TDEF page 33

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **1**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

### Section offsets (computed)

| Section | Start | Size | End (excl) |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Page header | 0 | 8 | 8 |
| TDEF block (Jet4: 55 bytes) | 8 | 55 | 63 |
| Real-idx skip entries (numRealIdx × 12) | 63 | 0 | 63 |
| Column descriptors (numCols × 25) | 63 | 25 | 88 |
| Column names (length-prefixed) | 88 | 12 | 100 |
| Variable trailing block (per-var-col page ptrs) | (after names) | (variable, terminated by col_num=0xFFFF) | — |

### Reason: complex-type template table (Jackcess `typeObjTable`)
## `MSysComplexType_Attachment` — TDEF page 39

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **4096**
- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **6**
- `num_idx` (offset 47, 4 bytes): **0**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **0**
- `ct_autonum` (Jet4 only, offset 28, 4 bytes): **0** — next ConceptualTableID for this table's complex columns

### Reason: hidden flat (child) table — `f_<guid>_<userColName>`

- `num_cols` (offset 45, 2 bytes): **8**

- `num_real_idx` (offset 51, 4 bytes): **3**
